==> default: exim4 (4.84.2-2) jessie; urgency=medium
==> default: 
==> default:   As part of the fix for CVE-2016-1531 updated Exim versions clean
==> default:   the complete execution environment by default, affecting Exim and
==> default:   subprocesses such as routers calling other programs, and thus may break
==> default:   existing installations. New configuration options (keep_environment,
==> default:   add_environment) were introduced to adjust this behavior. Because of the
==> default:   possible breakage Exim will show a runtime warning if keep_environment is
==> default:   not set.
==> default: 
==> default:   The Debian exim4 configuration does not rely on specific environment
==> default:   variables and therefore sets 'keep_environment =' (i.e confirm empty
==> default:   environment).
==> default: 
==> default:   Users of custom Exim configurations will need to check whether their setup
==> default:   continues to work with the abovementioned upstream change and modify the
==> default:   Exim environment as needed otherwise. If the setup works fine with empty
==> default:   environment it is still necessary to set the main configuration option
==> default:   "keep_environment =" to quiet the runtime warning.
==> default: 
==> default:   See <https://exim.org/static/doc/CVE-2016-1531.txt> for details.

exim4 (4.84.2-2) jessie; urgency=medium

  As part of the fix for CVE-2016-1531 updated Exim versions clean
  the complete execution environment by default, affecting Exim and
  subprocesses such as routers calling other programs, and thus may break
  existing installations. New configuration options (keep_environment,
  add_environment) were introduced to adjust this behavior. Because of the
  possible breakage Exim will show a runtime warning if keep_environment is
  not set.

  The Debian exim4 configuration does not rely on specific environment
  variables and therefore sets 'keep_environment =' (i.e confirm empty
  environment).

  Users of custom Exim configurations will need to check whether their setup
  continues to work with the abovementioned upstream change and modify the
  Exim environment as needed otherwise. If the setup works fine with empty
  environment it is still necessary to set the main configuration option
  "keep_environment =" to quiet the runtime warning.

  See <https://exim.org/static/doc/CVE-2016-1531.txt> for details.

 -- Andreas Metzler <ametzler@debian.org>  Mon, 28 Mar 2016 17:58:09 +0200
